title: "【宜蘭景點&美食懶人包】34個宜蘭景點+26家宜蘭美食，包含親子景點/情侶約會/住宿，一次通通報你知!(2023.07月更新)"
date: "2023-07-01T06:19:00.000Z"
cover: "/images/posts/12189377245/0.jpg"

<div class="pixnet-article prose max-w-none">
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="/tmp/phpAB5vmy" src="/images/posts/12189377245/0.jpg" alt="/tmp/phpAB5vmy" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #008080;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">宜蘭一日遊怎麼玩？</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">有哪些是必玩的景點推薦呢？！</span></span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #008080;">兩隻小豬今天就來分享宜蘭景點＆宜蘭美食，</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #008080;">不知道怎麼安排比較順路的話，</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #008080;">可以按著宜蘭同地區的景點玩，</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #008080;">或是依照自己喜好增減想去的地方，</span><span style="font-size: 16px; color: #008080;">規劃個一日遊或是二日遊的行程，</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #008080;">最後，祝大家都有美好愉快的假期囉～</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 16px;">近日收到網友詢問一日遊行程該如何規劃，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 16px;">所以決定簡單跟大家介紹幾個路線，方便納入參考喔</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">以兩隻小豬多次去宜蘭旅遊的經驗是建議<strong><span style="background-color: #ffff00; color: #0000ff;">搭乘客運</span></strong>會比較方便，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">從捷運市政府站(<span style="font-size: 16px;">捷運<span style="background-color: #0000ff; color: #ffffff;">板南線</span>往<strong><span style="color: #3366ff;">南港展覽館</span></strong>方向)</span>搭乘<strong>「<span style="color: #800000;">首都客運</span>」</strong>，價格約160元左右，車程約一小時內抵達。</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" src="http://www.post.gov.tw/post/FileCenter/post_ww2/post_docdata_att/att_content/0EBA3032-F089-47B7-A511-798C1E979F48/6CB6082D-6571-4145-90B1-91CBF2C2234A.bmp" alt="相關圖片" width="390" height="451">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">(圖片來源：網路)</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">
<script type="text/javascript">// <![CDATA[

// ]]></script>
<script src="http://kdpic.pchome.com.tw/img/js/xpcadshow.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">其實宜蘭地區算是蠻大，從礁溪到羅東約15-30分鐘車程，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">若是只有一日遊的話，</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">建議固定在同一區域慢慢玩就好~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">搭乘客運到宜蘭後，沒有開車的話，兩隻小豬</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">都是租機車(一台約400元)，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">可以找<span style="color: #ff0000;"><strong>羅東天天來租車行<span style="color: #000000;">，</span><span style="color: #0000ff;">地址:</span></strong></span></span><strong><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;">宜蘭縣羅東鎮黎明街40號</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">4-6人建議包小黃，網路查到的價格2000-5000元都有可能，依時間與距離不同價格不一。</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="羅東天天來租車行" src="/images/posts/12189377245/2.jpg" alt="羅東天天來租車行" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">因為和租車行是同學的關係，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">所以小豬特別為大家謀福利啦!!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">只要到<strong><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: #ff0000;">宜蘭羅東</span><span style="color: #ff0000; font-size: 14pt;">天天來租車行</span></strong>租車，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">至<span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><a href="https://www.facebook.com/twopiggyhavefun/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">兩隻小豬</span></a></span>、<span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="https://www.facebook.com/lotungtentenlike/?hc_ref=ARRwAbzaUQMmt0V4cRFGJR7M4tiV_Az0zdt1Bkkro8EZoQ5eHLCLM-yrRlZdxcd2mg4" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">租車行</span></a></span></span> FB粉絲團按讚，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: #ff00ff;"><strong>租車即可折價50元唷~~</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="font-size: 14pt; color: #0000ff;">租車有附贈</span>&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="background-color: #ffff99;">晶圓 包心粉圓</span>、</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; background-color: #ffcc99;">諾貝爾 奶凍折價券<span style="background-color: #ffffff;">和</span></span><span style="font-size: 12pt; background-color: #99ccff;">羅東夜市美食地圖</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong><span style="color: #ff0000;">【宜蘭市景點】</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="https://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/226614604" target="_blank"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">樂色山積木博物館，上千件積木作品~小小兵、巨無霸珍奶樂高等，必玩積木健康步道，還能動手組合樂高唷！</span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000;">宜蘭「樂色山」以積木為主題館在館內擺設上千個展品，每個作品都超震撼！不僅能欣賞多件積木作品，也可以自己動手組合樂高，甚至還能挑戰繽紛的積木健康步道大人和小朋友都玩得超開心，適合納入親子同遊的好地方~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><img loading="lazy" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/51879680630_e81537eb1d_c.jpg" alt="2022_0129_14361300"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a style="font-size: 12pt;" href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/224061483" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">CP Cheese Factory 超品起司烘焙工坊，各式起司糕點&amp;伴手禮</span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">這是一間以起司為主題的觀光工廠，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">除了販售各式起司糕點，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">還有超好拍的歐風大書牆📚</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">並設有咖啡用餐區☕</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">蠻適合納入雨天備案景點唷～</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/48947179202" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/48947179202_7666fd27a9_z.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1571547044399_mh1571547088086"></a></span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/211127140" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">幾米星空列車&amp;幸福轉運站，老舊車站變身夢幻「幾米世界」</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">來到宜蘭，除了到幾米公園拍拍照，還能走到對面的丟丟噹森林逛逛唷~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">「丟丟噹森林」位於宜蘭火車站正前方，現在作為百果樹藝文空間使用</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">「幸福轉運站」運用廢棄的公車，以長頸鹿和大象為主題，結合遊樂器材，還有盪鞦韆、溜滑梯等玩樂功能</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">宜蘭礁溪免費室內景點👉<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;">金車生技水產養殖研發中心</span></span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222513225" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">甲鳥園，清水模鴨舍建築好好拍，品嘗鴨蛋做成的鴨蛋糕及滷蛋~</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ffff99; color: #ff99cc;">宜蘭礁溪又有新景點啦~~</span>「甲鳥園」由傳統鴨寮轉型，打造清水模鴨舍建築</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">完全顛覆一般人對於鴨舍髒亂的刻板印象，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">來到這裡可以體驗生態之外，還可以買飼料餵鴨、餵魚~</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">並品嘗鴨蛋做成的鴨蛋糕及麵包等。　</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" title="IMG_2054" src="/images/posts/12189377245/8.jpg" alt="IMG_2054" border="0"></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/218445846" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">猴洞坑瀑布，俯瞰蘭陽地區美景，挑戰性0%</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">位在宜蘭的「猴洞坑瀑布」</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">從入口處到瀑布不用10分鐘路程，攻頂後就是一片清澈見底的溪水~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">還可眺望整片蘭陽平原，非常適合懶惰又想親近大自然的朋友們!!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" title="猴洞坑瀑布" src="/images/posts/12189377245/9.jpg" alt="猴洞坑瀑布" border="0"><span style="font-family: 微軟正黑體;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/164747068" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">礁溪湯圍溝溫泉魚主題文化館。快來給魚咬腳皮~~</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">每次來宜蘭礁溪玩，一定都會來礁溪湯圍溝溫泉魚主題文化館，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">這家位於湯圍溝公園內，往左邊那條走就會看到~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">泡腳費用大人80元，小孩60元，並附上擦腳巾，完全不限時間</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">裡面有分很多種等級的池，主要差別在於魚的大小，越大隻腳就越癢XD</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1446536367-1501260158_n" src="/images/posts/12189377245/10.jpg" alt="1446536367-1501260158_n" border="0"></span></p>

<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222492327" target="_blank"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">頭城濱海森林公園，八角瞭望台/旋轉樓梯交錯空間，復古氛圍好好拍!</span></a></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">說到<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 14pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff99cc;">宜蘭IG打卡熱點</span>，絕對少不了這個地方<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;">「頭城濱海森林公園」</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">斑駁的八角瞭望台，每一層樓都可以看到不同角度的海景，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">還有中空式的迴旋樓梯，不論從上往下拍或是從下方拍上去，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">都能拍出不同風格的美照喔!</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【冬山鄉景點】</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">伊格魯童話森林，5大必拍場景，就像走進童話森林國度！</span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff99cc;">宜蘭又有新景點可以拍透透囉～～</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000; background-color: #ffff99;">彩色房子、湖上透明冰屋和美人魚銅像，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ffff99;">搭配落羽松景觀，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ffff99;">根本超有北歐童話森林fu</span>🥰</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000;">室內還有繪本故事館及聖誕老人村，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000;">每個角落都佈置的超用心又有氣氛，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">拍完照還能到餐廳享用下午茶餐點，</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">放假就來趟偽北歐半日遊吧！</span></span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 1em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 1.1rem; line-height: 1.75rem; font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', 微軟正黑體, sans-serif; vertical-align: baseline; color: #343434; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/50897922512" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%; height: auto;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/50897922512_39ba6fdfef_c.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1612179799005"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/224000814" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">斑比山丘，近距離餵食梅花鹿好療癒，憑門票還可免費兌換飼料一份！</span></span></span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">💓宜蘭新景點👉<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;">斑比山丘</span>🦌</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">現在不用飛去日本也能在台灣近距離和小鹿互動啦😍😍</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">不僅能近距離餵食梅花鹿，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">還能體驗餵食的樂趣～</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">拍完照也能到小鹿紀念品區逛逛，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">或是到美美子咖啡館享用下午茶唷🍵</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/48841902816" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/48841902816_1e307a1177_z.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1569812231900_mh1569830220347"></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration-line: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222538101" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff;">仁山植物園，歐式庭園景觀好好拍，偶爾走走享受芬多精也不錯(免費入園)</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">發現宜蘭也有一座世外桃源，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">「仁山植物園」全程約三公里，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">終點是一個視野寬闊的觀景平台，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">很適合吃飽後散步、享受芬多精的好地方🍃</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/43213347240" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1968/43213347240_75d6774496_z.jpg" alt="仁山植物園 (1)"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/216993296" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">龍座咖啡、輕食、下午茶，絕美的雙心石滬景觀餐廳，一眼望去景色遼闊!</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">位於宜蘭冬山的「龍座咖啡」，真的是一個很放鬆的地方!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">不用到澎湖就能看到絕美的「雙心石滬」、「I love you」的造景，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">讓人感覺身處在世外桃源，不論是約會、喝下午茶、拍照，都很合適唷~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="page" src="/images/posts/12189377245/18.jpg" alt="page" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/189650512" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">廣興農場-鴨母寮豬哥窟，適合親子出遊的景點</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span>園區內不只可以體驗農村生活之外，</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span>還有可愛的動物、DIY體驗、益智遊戲、焢窯、兒時遊戲等等，</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><span>而且到處都是玩樂遊戲的玩意兒，讓人再度重溫兒時的童趣!!</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="IMG_20160209_214450_908" src="/images/posts/12189377245/19.jpg" alt="IMG_20160209_214450_908" border="0"></span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【五結鄉景點】</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/216041258" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">綠舞觀光飯店&amp;綠舞日式主題園區，日式庭園設計超好拍~</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">位於宜蘭五結鄉的「綠舞國際觀光飯店」，是全台唯一結合日式庭園、飯店和獨棟Villa的五星級國際觀光飯店~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">其中日式庭園的綠舞日式主題園區已經開放</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">讓遊客遊玩囉~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">園區內以日式庭園景觀為主，設有水濂洞、美術館、輕食館、展演館等主題空間，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">不用出國就能在這感受到濃濃的日本味💖</span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="20170407213641_org" src="/images/posts/12189377245/21.jpg" alt="20170407213641_org" border="0"></span></p>

<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;">&nbsp;</h2>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【蘇澳景點】</span></strong></h2>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;">&nbsp;</h2>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration-line: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/218354760" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">南方澳觀景台，360度觀海平台，真是美炸了!</span></a></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">「南方澳觀景台」是位在蘇花公路108公里處，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">站在觀景台可以飽覽台灣東北海岸的美景，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">跟小編一樣愛看海的人，絕對不能錯過!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ff0000; font-size: 12pt;"><strong><span style="text-decoration-line: underline;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><img loading="lazy" src="/images/posts/12189377245/23.jpg" alt="南方澳02.jpg"></span></span></strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" src="/images/posts/12189377245/24.jpg" alt="南方澳03.jpg"></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/216172910" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">海洋20M海景咖啡館，藍白地中海裝潢，遠眺遼闊海景~</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">這次的宜蘭二日遊，特別造訪南方澳漁港附近的「海洋20M海景咖啡館」，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">除了具有地中海風的建築，還能欣賞美麗遼闊的海景，適合在這放鬆度過一下午~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="海洋20M海景咖啡館" src="/images/posts/12189377245/25.jpg" alt="海洋20M海景咖啡館" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration-line: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a style="color: #020202; text-decoration: underline;" href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/189265234" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">祝大漁物產文創館。360度3D海底隧道，彷彿置身海底世界~~</span></a></span></span></span></h2>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">「祝大漁物產文創館」最讓人驚豔的就是360度3D海底隧道，</span></h2>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">彷彿置身在海底世界~也難怪吸引不少遊客前來朝聖，</span></h2>
<h2 style="font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: normal; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">而且免收門票費，還有廣場可供停車~</span></h2>

<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; line-height: 20px; text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #000000;">(若要單點燈泡珍奶，下午3點30分後供應)</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 18pt;"><span style="text-decoration-line: underline;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【三星鄉景點】</span></strong></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222097455" target="_blank"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">安農溪分洪堰風景區，安農溪水門一分為二，湍急河流水聲，拍出震撼臨場感</span></a></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">雖然這時候來不是落羽松季節，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">但整座綠意盎然的景色也是很好拍💖</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">水門兩側就是綠油油草地，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">加上當天天氣陰涼，整條走起來很舒服，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">適合吃飽飯後來這裡散步、拍照~</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/42966508492" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/875/42966508492_8fbab28e78_z.jpg" alt="安農溪分洪堰風景區 (1)"></a></p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【大同鄉景點】</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/223375437" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">棲蘭神木園，亞洲最大檜木神木園，也是賽德克巴萊拍攝場景之一~</span></span></span></span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12pt;">這次來到棲蘭神木園完全讓人大開眼界，</span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">近百棵千年以上的紅檜與台灣扁柏矗立園區，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12pt;">而且每一顆神木名字都是以歷代古聖先賢來命名，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 12pt;">像是：陶淵明、司馬遷和諸葛亮等等．．．</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;步道</span><span style="font-size: 12pt;">設有長、短程環行步道，可以衡量自己身體狀況選擇~</span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline; color: #35a3ca; text-align: center;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/40711030773" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/40711030773_3bc5d51293_z.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1556023700236"></a></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/211686292" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">清水地熱公園，體驗用泉水煮溫泉蛋、玉米，還可至泡湯池暖暖腳！&nbsp;</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">除了可以體驗用泉水煮食溫泉蛋、玉米等，一旁還設有泡湯區供遊客泡腳(40~42度左右)，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">既可以溫暖心又能填飽胃，是個適合帶全家大小出遊的好地方！</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="27" src="/images/posts/12189377245/31.jpg" alt="27" border="0"></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="IMG_0539" src="/images/posts/12189377245/32.jpg" alt="IMG_0539" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【員山鄉景點】</span></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">可達休閒羊場，免門票小型農場，餵羊咩咩喝奶/吃牧草/餵兔子吃紅蘿蔔</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">🐏<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff9900;">宜蘭超推的農場</span>👉<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #99cc00;">可達休閒羊場</span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">雖然整個農場的佔地不大，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">但比起其他熱門的農場，這裡幽靜許多😍</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">而且100元套票就能餵小羊喝奶、餵大羊吃牧草、餵鴨子吃飼料和餵兔子吃紅蘿蔔！</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">結束後還能兌換羊奶系列的點心，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">整體CP值蠻高的唷💕</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444; text-align: center;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/48929411062" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/48929411062_48a229ae51_z.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1571120395092"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">勝洋休閒農場，增設釣魚、魚咬腳皮、划竹筏體驗，門口還有好拍的彩虹傘！</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">相隔四年再到<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff9900;">勝洋休閒農場</span>，發現這裡新增了好多休閒設施✨</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">像是：釣魚、魚咬腳皮、划竹筏及拉水壩體驗，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">門口還有好拍的彩虹傘😍</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">園內也有提供輕食和飲品，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">來這享受大自然生態環境還蠻不錯！</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline; color: #444444; text-align: center;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/48754038651" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/48754038651_0e870a8a3e_z.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1568809308551"></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222106764" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">香草菲菲芳香植物博物館，天空步道伴隨陣陣花香，下午茶飲品可無限暢飲!</span></a></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">算一算和小豬來香草菲菲很多次了，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">每次來都覺得天空步道超好拍😍</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">尤其是整棟白色溫室建築，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">舒適的環境，伴隨著陣陣花香～🌺</span><span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; font-style: inherit; font-variant-ligatures: inherit; font-variant-caps: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">讓人感覺很放鬆！</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/43009815132" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm1.staticflickr.com/835/43009815132_0851509852_z.jpg" alt="香草菲菲 (27)"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/29187653898" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1824/29187653898_94b4945222_z.jpg" alt="香草菲菲 (38)"></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/218016438" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;">A.maze兔子迷宮景觀咖啡餐廳，絕美的彩虹天空步道，180度眺望蘭陽平原!</span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">來到宜蘭首座天空步道的兔子迷宮，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">不僅有絕美的彩虹天空步道，還可以180度眺望蘭陽平原，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">一眼望去的視野相當遼闊，美景盡收眼底，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">除了適合情侶同遊，也是親子景點的好去處喔~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/album/photo/115322913"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" title="A.maze兔子迷宮36.jpg" src="/images/posts/12189377245/37.jpg" alt="A.maze兔子迷宮36.jpg" border="0"></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><strong style="color: #ff0000; font-size: 12pt;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/album/photo/115322892"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" title="A.maze兔子迷宮30.jpg" src="/images/posts/12189377245/38.jpg" alt="A.maze兔子迷宮30.jpg" border="0"></a></strong></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/album/photo/115322901"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" title="A.maze兔子迷宮33.jpg" src="/images/posts/12189377245/39.jpg" alt="A.maze兔子迷宮33.jpg" border="0"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/216935858" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;">金車蘭花園，北台灣最大型的專業蘭園，雨天備案景點!(全年無休，免費入園)</span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">金車蘭花園為北台灣最大的專業蘭園，佔地面積八千五百四十坪，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">因為宜蘭地區氣候潮濕多雨，非常適合養蘭的栽培，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">擁有規模相當龐大的溫室，年產多達二百五十萬株左右之蝴蝶蘭，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">而且目前全年無休，適合當作雨天備案景點喔!!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" src="/images/posts/12189377245/40.jpg" alt="金車蘭花園49.JPG">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" src="/images/posts/12189377245/41.jpg" alt="金車蘭花園39.JPG"></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" src="/images/posts/12189377245/42.jpg" alt="金車蘭花園31.JPG"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/174663532" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">養蜂人家-蜂采館。全國唯一蜜蜂生態博物館</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">這家養蜂人家 蜂采館位於宜蘭員山，是一間以蜜蜂為主題的景點~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">館內也有賣許多蜂蜜產品，例如:蜂蜜蛋糕、龍眼蜜、蜂王乳、蜂蜜醋等等。</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1447302499-507904948_n (1)" src="/images/posts/12189377245/43.jpg" alt="1447302499-507904948_n (1)" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<hr>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【宜蘭美食】</span></strong></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a href="https://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/226523101" target="_blank">【宜蘭礁溪親子餐廳】水鹿咖啡親子館，餐點多樣化，設有溜滑梯.沙坑.盪鞦韆及小火車，還可近距離餵食小動物喔！</a></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">時隔幾年再次造訪「水鹿咖啡親子館」，發現搬家後變化好大啊~餐點多樣化之外，還增設一區兒童遊樂區和可愛動物區，有溜滑梯.沙坑.盪鞦韆及小火車，小朋友玩得超開心😆還可買飼料近距離餵食小動物，另外，室內用餐區限時兩小時，而室外兒童遊樂區就不限時，所以想玩多久都可以，非常適合當作親子用餐的地方唷~</span></p>
<p><img loading="lazy" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/51877163304_bcb9c3bb42_c.jpg" alt="uri_mh1644115709785"></p>
<p><img loading="lazy" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/51877164454_fb9c7c374b_c.jpg" alt="uri_mh1644114205281"></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a href="https://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/225809258" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline;">【宜蘭蘭城晶英烤鴨】紅樓中餐廳，一鴨五吃超經典，最愛櫻桃鴨握壽司!(附最新菜單.餐點表現)</span></span></span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">蘭城晶英的烤鴨真的太好吃啦( ⸝⸝⸝⁼̴́◡⁼̴̀⸝⸝⸝)​</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">從開胃菜、櫻桃鴨、海鮮、湯品到甜點都好喜歡​，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">獨創吃法 一鴨五吃真的很厲害耶​!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">其中「櫻桃鴨握壽司」實在讓人一吃上癮~​</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">其他菜色：片皮鴨捲三星蔥餅、生菜包鴨絲、慢火白菜煲鴨湯也很有特色​，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">多樣菜色適合家庭聚餐或是相約朋友一起吃​，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">如果你也喜歡吃烤鴨​，真的覺得可以試試！！​</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline;"><img loading="lazy" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/51854179548_d44c3957bd_c.jpg" alt="SNOW_20220131_211536_632"></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline;">望龍埤鵝肉攤，鵝湯麵/鵝湯米粉/白飯吃到飽:每人只要$20元，菜色新鮮美味!</span></span></span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">宜蘭望龍埤附近有間鵝肉攤，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">真是佛心來著🤩😍</span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">竟然提供👉<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 14pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;">鵝湯麵/鵝湯米粉/白飯吃到飽<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #000000;">，</span></span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">每人只要$20元</span>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">餐點價格實惠之外，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">這次點的炒菜類都蠻好吃的，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">調味也剛剛好、不會太油或太鹹，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">吃飽還能到附近的望龍碑走走～</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline;"><img loading="lazy" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/50214104417_6b2940d032_z.jpg" alt="IMG_20200614_120852"></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="https://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/224840658" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration: underline;">礁溪甕窯雞(蘭陽礁溪總店)，宜蘭排隊名店甕窯雞，附設免費停車場!</span></span></a></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">在頭城礁溪交流道下有一家人氣爆棚的甕窯雞，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">假日幾乎是滿滿的用餐人潮，環境空間也非常寬敞，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">餐點除了有香氣誘人的烤雞，還有多種合菜料理，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">好適合多人來聚餐！</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">&nbsp;<a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/50015908588" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/50015908588_f2b63e5f74_z.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1592408458905"></a></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="https://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/224393250" target="_blank"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">愛烤愛對囉-宜蘭店，各式韓式烤豬五花、和牛、海鮮吃到飽，還有桌邊烤肉服務!</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">這次來宜蘭吃到一間很不錯的燒烤吃到飽，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">食材種類多元、品質新鮮之外，</span></p>
