<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">位於宜蘭員山的「漁樂釣魚碳烤休閒餐廳」</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">用餐消費滿$800元即可免費釣魚，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">還會依人數給你釣魚竿、吐司，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">是一個適合聚餐又可休閒娛樂的好地方!</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/45022044851" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1949/45022044851_d15081d61c_z.jpg" alt="【宜蘭員山餐廳漁樂釣魚碳烤休閒餐廳"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222513993" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">解憂商號(沒來吃粥 渾身不自在)，超澎湃痛風粥滿滿10幾隻鮮蝦＋2隻天使紅蝦，還有一整隻完整的螃蟹</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">這次來宜蘭玩終於讓我吃到這家👉<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 14pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;">解憂商號</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">食材新鮮之外，還可依照自己的預算選擇配料，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">基本款海鮮粥都有蝦子、蛤蜊、花枝及鮮蚵，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">最便宜只要１００元，絕對是海鮮控的天堂呀！</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/44903124191" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1974/44903124191_46eca1ab8c_z.jpg" alt="解憂商號(沒來吃粥 渾身不自在) (15)"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222497469" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">來來牛排館，蒜香脆皮雞排超對味，餐點均附脆皮濃湯、沙拉及甜點</span></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">假日生意好到爆炸的「來來牛排館」</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">餐點均附脆皮濃湯、沙拉及甜點，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">義大利麵加量不加價，還有免費紅茶無限續，不收服務費，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">可以說是CP值超高的店阿~</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/29860412027" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1848/29860412027_4403d3af36_z.jpg" alt="宜蘭來來牛排館 10"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration-line: underline;">佐佐清水自家烘焙咖啡館(生態綠舟店)</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">「佐佐清水自家烘焙咖啡館」環境舒適之外，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">以平實的價格就能吃到手工製作的甜點!</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">而且每種甜點一片不到$100元!!!</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">好想自己收藏在口袋名單阿~ ( 笑 )</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/44754497621" target="_blank"><span style="color: #000000;"><img loading="lazy" style="border-width: initial; border-style: none; margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1885/44754497621_87a2a37c9c_z.jpg" alt="佐佐清水自家烘焙咖啡館(生態綠洲店) (46)"></span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/222101406" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">番割田甕缸雞，肉質鮮嫩不乾柴，沾上雞油食用更讚!</span></a></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">「番割田甕缸雞」用餐空間舒適，送餐速度快，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">這次點的餐點沒有讓人覺得雷，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">尤其是甕缸雞絕對是來這裡必點，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">肉質鮮嫩不乾柴，再搭配一旁雞油一起吃，整個超讚!!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">是一間適合家人.朋友聚餐的餐廳!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" title="IMG_6833" src="/images/posts/12189377245/58.jpg" alt="IMG_6833" border="0"><span style="font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/217858536" target="_blank"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">小島日和，季節限定芒果冰，整面浪漫花牆超好拍！</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">這次點的夏季芒果冰我們都蠻喜歡，口感香甜又沁涼!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">店內環境也很舒適，除了最大亮點的花牆，天花板還有用乾燥花裝飾，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">整個環境氛圍讓人很放鬆，難怪深受大家喜愛!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">而且離羅東夜市也很近，吃完剛好去逛夜市續攤</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff0000;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">每人低消：</span>$100元，不收服務費</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/211074433" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">海世界複合式碳烤，超澎湃海鮮自助燒烤，牡蠣新鮮又大顆!!</span></span></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">超澎湃海鮮自助燒烤，光是整條魚下去烤就佔烤網一半面積~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">牡蠣也是很新鮮大顆，喜歡大魚大肉的人別錯過這家摟~</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/212410045" target="_blank"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">「熊飽鍋物」主題式涮涮鍋店，熊熊主題親子餐廳萌萌噠!</span></span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">位在宜蘭運動公園旁的熊飽鍋物，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">除了有可愛的熊熊娃娃擺設，並設置兒童遊戲區，讓吃飽的孩子可以在一旁玩</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">餐點提供多種湯頭外，也有各式海鮮和肉片，價格約在中價位，適合帶著全家大小前往~</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">雖然網路上很多人介紹米苔目，但實際吃完會比較推薦大家點碗粿，</span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/213650668" target="_blank">老街懷舊食堂，椒麻雞腿飯/當歸湯/天霸王滷肉飯，滿滿的濃厚古早味!</a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="IMG_20161025_212256_578" src="/images/posts/12189377245/67.jpg" alt="IMG_20161025_212256_578" border="0"></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="IMG_20161025_212446_560" src="/images/posts/12189377245/68.jpg" alt="IMG_20161025_212446_560" border="0"></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="IMG_20161025_212420_881" src="/images/posts/12189377245/69.jpg" alt="IMG_20161025_212420_881" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><br><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/216910463" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">龍記牛肉麵，牛肉、牛筋軟嫩紮實，超有飽足感!</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">看起來小小一碗的筋肉麵，其實份量十足!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">裡面牛筋約莫4大塊，牛筋燉煮的非常軟嫩，帶點黏稠的膠質感</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">湯頭喝起來甘甜，帶點淡淡中藥香氣，以及水果香甜</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/album/photo/106893489"><img loading="lazy" title="龍記牛肉麵19.JPG" src="/images/posts/12189377245/70.jpg" alt="龍記牛肉麵19.JPG" border="0"></a></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/album/photo/106893483"><img loading="lazy" title="龍記牛肉麵17.JPG" src="/images/posts/12189377245/71.jpg" alt="龍記牛肉麵17.JPG" border="0"></a> &nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/category/3883591" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">【湯蒸火鍋】在地人推薦的高CP值火鍋店</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">來到湯蒸火鍋開車的話不用怕找不到停車位，位於店家後方就有停車場唷~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">第一次來宜蘭吃湯蒸火鍋覺得還不錯，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">而且最後還有送上甜點-綠豆湯，冰冰涼涼的蠻好喝~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">重點是這邊的蔬菜盤都很新鮮，竟然有別家火鍋店沒有附的魚漿丸~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="page" src="/images/posts/12189377245/72.jpg" alt="page" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/189274486" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">樂山溫泉拉麵。礁溪泡腳拉麵創始店，強棒拉麵料多豐富</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">樂山溫泉拉麵價格算平價，拉麵價位大約在$80~$250元，而且吃完非常有飽足感~</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; line-height: 20px; text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1454742393-3441079649" src="/images/posts/12189377245/73.jpg" alt="1454742393-3441079649" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; line-height: 20px; text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1454742393-1764622385_n" src="/images/posts/12189377245/74.jpg" alt="1454742393-1764622385_n" border="0"> &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: #777777; font-family: arial; letter-spacing: 1px; line-height: 20px; text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/165872218" target="_blank"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">合鴨米灶腳。在地人也愛吃的平民美食</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">「合鴨米灶腳」離礁溪湯圍溝主題館非常近唷~就在另一條巷內而已!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1446627136-3535732218_n" src="/images/posts/12189377245/75.jpg" alt="1446627136-3535732218_n" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1446627136-4103114902_n" src="/images/posts/12189377245/76.jpg" alt="1446627136-4103114902_n" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline; font-size: 12pt;"><img loading="lazy" title="1446627136-4275956980_n" src="/images/posts/12189377245/77.jpg" alt="1446627136-4275956980_n" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/216289445" target="_blank"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">原來豆花，黑糖綿綿冰+豆花，這樣吃也幸福!</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">位於宜蘭的「原來豆花」，超大碗任選三種料才40元，可惜目前已漲價成50元</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">豆花除了可選三種配料，上方還搭配一顆紅棗、一杯煉乳，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">而且配料是和豆花分開裝，就像是一個套餐~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">不論是想吃冰豆花或是熱甜品，都非常適合喔!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="原來豆花" src="/images/posts/12189377245/78.jpg" alt="原來豆花" border="0"> &nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 18pt;"><strong style="font-size: 18.6667px;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">【宜蘭住宿】</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">卡布雷莊園民宿，裝潢精美超華麗，房間還有巧虎溜滑梯球池，小孩玩瘋了!</span></span></strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">宜蘭超華麗的親子民宿，推薦給你們!</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">這次入住歐式建築風格的民宿-<span style="color: #993300;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;" href="http://www.cabremanor.tw/" rel="nofollow ugc noreferrer noopener" target="_blank"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #993300;">卡布雷莊園</span></a></span>，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">從大廳、房間到用餐區都佈置的好用心<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">，</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">很像住進歐洲皇宮城堡(ෆˊ͈ ु꒳ ूˋ͈ෆ)</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">房間內也有溜滑梯、球池及廚房玩具<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">，</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">小孩玩得超開心😆</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">而且浴室一樣延續歐式裝潢<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">，</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">各種盥洗都有提供，也有浴缸可以泡澡<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">，還有超跑電動車，讓小孩玩瘋了~~</span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">如果你也喜歡歐洲風的親子民宿，那麼，這間會很適合你喔!</span></span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">週末就來這歐洲城堡住一晚吧!</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;"><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/51861267841" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/51861267841_cdb1a1497a_c.jpg" alt="InShot_20220204_165252386"></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="https://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/225234341" target="_blank"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">&nbsp;麗筑藝術親子民宿，親子房溜滑梯設計，設有兒童遊戲間/開放式廚房/陽台空間，附免費早餐!</span></a></span></strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">每間房間有不同主題之外，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">親子房還有<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">溜滑梯設計</span>～</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 1em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 1.1rem; line-height: 1.75rem; font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', 微軟正黑體, sans-serif; vertical-align: baseline; color: #343434; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ffff99;">兒童遊戲區</span>也相當豐富，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">有小火車、積木桌、辦家家酒玩具和兒童電動車等等</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 1em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 1.1rem; line-height: 1.75rem; font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', 微軟正黑體, sans-serif; vertical-align: baseline; color: #343434; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">可以讓孩子們盡情放電😆</span></p>
<p style="margin: 1em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 1.1rem; line-height: 1.75rem; font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', 微軟正黑體, sans-serif; vertical-align: baseline; color: #343434; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">而且民宿有電梯設計，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">就算行李爆多也不用爬樓梯上下搬，</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 1em 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 1.1rem; line-height: 1.75rem; font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', 微軟正黑體, sans-serif; vertical-align: baseline; color: #343434; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">距離<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: bold; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">傳藝中心</span>也很近，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 12pt; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">適合當作順遊景點唷～</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; font-size: 17.6px; line-height: inherit; font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', 微軟正黑體, sans-serif; vertical-align: baseline; letter-spacing: 1px; text-align: center;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/50908086446" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; font: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%; height: auto;" src="https://live.staticflickr.com/65535/50908086446_715b62c75e_c.jpg" alt="PhotoGrid_1612441374653"></a></p>

<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">宜蘭五結</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">「夏沐雷民宿」</span></span>不只有許多房型可選擇，</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; font-size: 12pt;">民宿建築外觀、<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">迎賓大廳</span>和房間</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">都打造的很溫馨，</span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">一早還能吃到民宿主人親手做的早餐，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">更棒的是，有我愛的浴缸可以泡澡放鬆♨️</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">而且距離<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #99cc00;">冬山河親水公園</span>也很近，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline; color: #008080;">放假就來<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">夏沐雷放鬆度假吧～</span></span>&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">這次宜蘭二日遊我們住在👉<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff6600;">天使輕旅．礁溪溫泉</span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">地理位置很方便，距離礁溪火車站僅 5 分鐘車程～</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">房內基本設備通通都有，42吋液晶電視、乾溼分離的衛浴，</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">還有雙人溫泉浴缸♨，並供應免費早餐！</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-variant-east-asian: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; font-size: 16px; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><a style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; text-decoration-line: none; color: #444444;" href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/158881690@N04/43110947100" target="_blank"><img loading="lazy" style="margin: 10px 0px; padding: 0px; border-width: initial; border-style: none; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; max-width: 100%;" src="https://farm2.staticflickr.com/1903/43110947100_dd9ce0b8ed_z.jpg" alt="天使輕旅 礁溪溫泉 Angels' Inn (1)"></a></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span style="color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;"><a href="http://lolwarden.pixnet.net/blog/post/219763278" target="_blank"><span style="font-size: 12pt; color: #0000ff; text-decoration: underline;">【宜蘭住宿】山口溫泉飯店，露天超大檜木SPA池，天冷泡湯去!(鄰近礁溪火車站)</span></a></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">兩隻小豬上回到宜蘭玩，就是住這間<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #993300;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">"山口溫泉飯店"</span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">距離礁溪火車站只要1.3公里，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">對於沒有開車的朋友來說，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">入住相當方便喔!</span></p>
<p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-variant-numeric: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: 微軟正黑體; vertical-align: baseline; text-align: left;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">房間舒適之外，</span><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-size: 12pt; vertical-align: baseline;">還有個<span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline; color: #ff0000;"><span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; vertical-align: baseline;">露天泡湯檜木池</span></span>，非常適合這種冷天來泡一下啊~~</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><img loading="lazy" title="山口溫泉飯店 (13)" src="/images/posts/12189377245/85.jpg" alt="山口溫泉飯店 (13)" border="0">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">雖然整理出來的好玩景點、好吃美食不是很多， </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">不過都會再陸續更新唷<img loading="lazy" src="https://s.pixfs.net/f.pixnet.net/images/emotions/017.gif" alt="【宜蘭景點&美食懶人包】34個宜蘭景點+26家宜蘭美食，包含親子景點/情侶約會/住宿，一次通通報你知!(2023.07月更新) - 兩隻小豬" border="0"></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">由於兩隻小豬每次到宜蘭出遊都會遇到下雨，</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 12pt;">以上分享的這些景點完全是雨天的備案行程阿~~&nbsp;</span></p>
